					<h2 id="mainHeading">Pitney Bowes Software Technical Services</h2>
					
					
								<div class="userMessage withRightFloat alert">
								<p>You're not yet authenticated. Please authenticate yourself using the form below. Unavailable items are <span class="unavailable">greyed out</span>. </p><p><em>* Both fields are required.</em></p>

					    <div class="clearer clearL""></div>
						<dl id="mainMenu">
							<dt><a class="unavailable" href="/Support/Products/">My Products</a></dt>
							<dd>Detailed information including software components, databases, product updates, license files, related documentation and more.</dd>	
								
							<dt><a href="http://www.g1.com/docs/LICASSIST.ZIP" title="Open ZIP in New Window" class="newwin popup zip">License Assist Utility for US Geocoding - Centrus and MapMarker USA</a></dt>
							<dd>This utility provides a file containing environmental information for use in generating a license file for Centrus products and MapMarker.</dd>
							
							<dt><a class="unavailable" href="/Support/Docs/">Documentation</a></dt>
							<dd>Users manuals, release notes, installation instructions and more.</dd>
	
							<dt><a class="unavailable" href="/Support/Products/dpvlacsnav.asp">DPV &amp; LACS<sup>Link</sup> False-Positive (Seed Violation) Recovery</a></dt>
							<dd>Use this page to locate the appropriate links to retrieve your replacement DPV&trade; and LACS<sup>Link</sup>&trade; license key files.</dd>	
	
							<dt><a href="/Support/SRD/">Special Request Downloads</a></dt>
							<dd>This area is for our customers who have been given a special download code by a technical support representative.</dd>
						
							<dt><a class="offsite popup" href="http://www.pbsoftwareforum.com">Online Discussion Forums</a></dt>
							<dd>We’ve updated our discussion forums. If you're looking for a place to talk with other Pitney Bowes Software customers, ask each other questions or share ideas &mdash; then this is the place to be. While Pitney Bowes Software does monitor these forums, they should not be used as a technical support option. If you are seeking technical support, please use our  <a href="/Support/online-case-management.asp" class="eservice unavailable">Online Case Management</a> feature.</dd>
							
							<dt><a class="unavailable" href="/Support/Contact/">Contact Information</a></dt>
							<dd>Need to get in touch with someone in Technical Services? Use this page as a handy reference for contacting the various departments in Pitney Bowes Software&rsquo;s Technical Services division.  Most entries include an email address, phone number, and a fax number.</dd>
							
							<dt><a href="/Support/Platform/" title="Supported Platforms" >Supported Platforms</a></dt>
							<dd>A listing of the supported platforms and operating systems our products support along with available delivery media.</dd>
							
							<dt><a class="unavailable" href="Help/">Support Site Help</a></dt>
							<dd>Answers to your questions regarding this section of the web site.</dd>			
							
							<dt><a class="unavailable" href="/Support/FTP/"><abbr title="File Transfer Protocol">FTP</abbr> Access</a></dt>
							<dd>Share files with Pitney Bowes Software using FTP. The FTP server is located at supportftp.g1.com for direct login with existing accounts.</dd>
				
							<dt><a class="unavailable" href="/Support/Forms/">Online Forms</a></dt>
							<dd>Many of the forms that you need are conveniently located right here. Need additional hardcopy documentation? Perhaps you want to suggest a product enhancement request. Simply complete the form that meets your needs and we'll respond as soon as possible.</dd>
				
							<dt><a href="/Support/online-case-management.asp">Online Case Management</a></dt>
							<dd>The new Online Case Management System provides similar functionality as the previous eService system but allows us more flexibility to provide a much richer online experience.</dd>
							<dd> 
								<div id="notification" class="userMessage">
									<h3>If you are in Canada</h3>
									<p>The enhanced online experience is now live! Select the appropriate Canadian "Sign in here" from <a href="http://www.pitneybowes.com/softwaresupport">www.pitneybowes.com/softwaresupport</a> to access the new enhanced online experience.</p>
									<p>Previous users of our Online Case Management tool in Canada should use the above link to register for a new account. Your previous Online Case Management credentials are not valid in the new enhanced online experience.</p>
									<h3>Everyone outside of Canada</h3>
									<p>All other clients will continue to login to the OCMS below. Our evolution to the enhanced online experience is a global rollout that will occur throughout 2016, therefore, clients may not have all products available until all geographies are live.</p>
									<p><a href="https://na6.salesforce.com/secur/login_portal.jsp?orgId=00D80000000KkyB&portalId=060800000006CN4">https://na6.salesforce.com/secur/login_portal.jsp?orgId=00D80000000KkyB&portalId=060800000006CN4</a></p>
								</div>
							</dd>
														
							<dt><a class="unavailable" href="/Support/Glossary/" title="Glossaries">Glossaries</a></dt>
							<dd>Glossaries of terms and definitions related to our products.</dd>
						
							<dt><a href="http://www.pbinsight.com/blog/" title="Pitney Bowes Software Blog (New Window)" onclick="window.open(this.href,'newwin'); return false;" class="newwin">PBS Blog</a></dt>
							<dd>An online resource for Pitney Bowes Software's leadership to share innovations, goals, and product/solution news and roadmaps, as well as exchange ideas with visitors. (<strong><a href="login.asp">Log in</a> first to unlock customer-only features!</strong>)</dd>
				
							<dt><a href="/Email/">List Services</a></dt>
							<dd>Use our List Services system to manage your Pitney Bowes Software email newsletter and other email based communications.</dd>
						
							<dt><a class="unavailable" href="/Support/Contact/ContactInfoForm.asp?updovr=y">Update Contact Info</a></dt>
							<dd>Use this link to request updates to your Contact profile. Your request will be processed by an associate and should appear on your Contact profile shortly.</dd>
							
						
						</dl>
